<script>
	if (document.location.pathname === "/") {

		function makeSameHeight(e) {

			var _boxes = document.getElementsByClassName('offsetbox');
			// for this page we don't do this for mobile
			if (window.innerWidth < 900) {

				for (var i = 0; i < _boxes.length; i++) {
					_boxes[i].style.height = "initial";
				}

				// exit since it is mobile, don't resize
				return;
			}

			var tallest = 0;
			// find tallest

			for (var i = 0; i < _boxes.length; i++) {
				// first get initial heights
				_boxes[i].style.height = "initial";
				// then check for tallest
				if (_boxes[i].offsetHeight > tallest) {
					tallest = _boxes[i].offsetHeight;
				}
			}


			// now apply tallest height to all
			for (var i = 0; i < _boxes.length; i++) {
				_boxes[i].style.height = String(tallest + 96) + "px";
			}

			var _bottomstick = document.getElementsByClassName('bottomstick');

			for (var i = 0; i < _bottomstick.length; i++) {
				_bottomstick[i].style.width = String(document.getElementsByClassName('innerlist')[0].offsetWidth) + "px";
			}
		
		} makeSameHeight();
	}
</script>

<script>
    // Read More
    // Scroll & Tracking Action
    if ($(".readmore").length > 0) {

        // Get Page Link
        var getPageLink  = $('link[rel="canonical"]').attr('href'),
            counter = 0;
        // Scroll
        $(window).on("scroll", function() {

            if ($(window).scrollTop() < $('.readmore').eq(0).offset().top && counter == 1)
                counter = -1;

            if (counter == -1) {
                history.replaceState('', '', getPageLink);
                nextPageTrackingAction(window.location.pathname);
                counter = 0;
			}

            if($(window).scrollTop() > $('.readmore').eq(0).offset().top && counter == 0) {
                if (counter == 0) {
                    history.replaceState('', '', getPageLink + '/?detay=1');
                    nextPageTrackingAction(window.location.pathname + "detay=1");
            		counter++;
                } else {
                    history.replaceState('', '', getPageLink);
                    nextPageTrackingAction(window.location.pathname);
				}
            }else if (typeof $('.readmore').eq(1).offset() !== "undefined" && $(window).scrollTop() > $('.readmore').eq(1).offset().top && counter == 1) {
				if (counter == 1) {
                    history.replaceState('', '', getPageLink + '/?detay=2');
                    nextPageTrackingAction(window.location.pathname + "detay=2");
                    counter++;
				}
            } else if (typeof $('.readmore').eq(1).offset() !== "undefined" && $(window).scrollTop() < $('.readmore').eq(1).offset().top && counter == 2){
                if(counter == 2) {
                    history.replaceState('', '', getPageLink);
                    nextPageTrackingAction(window.location.pathname);
                    counter=0;
                }
            }
        });

		// Readmore After
		// Empty Paragraph Fix
        $('.readmore').each(function(e) {
            if($(' + p', this).html().length < 2) {
                $(' + p', this).hide();
            }
        });
    }

    // Next Page
    // Tracking Action
    function nextPageTrackingAction(triggerAnalyticsUrl, defaultTitle) {

    }

              $(document).ready(function(){
                var url_base = "https://www.elsalvador.com/wp-json/LoadMore/v1/getTopHotTrend";

                function loadTopContent(type){
                  $.ajax({
                    url: url_base + "/" + type,
                    method: "GET",
                    dataType: "json"
                  }).done(function(data){
                  	 switch(type){
                  	   case 1:
                  	           $("#top-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;
                  	   case 2:
                  	           $("#hot-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;
                  	   case 3:
                  	           $("#trending-content-box").html(data);
                  	           break;   	
                  	 }
                  }).fail(function(jqXHR, textStatus, errorThrown){
                     console.log("Error al obtener las notas del top: " + JSON.stringify(jqXHR));
                  });
                }

                loadTopContent(1);
                  
                $("#hot-link").on("click
336
", function(){
                   if(!$.trim($("#hot-content-box").html())){
                     loadTopContent(2);
                   }	
                });

                     loadTopContent(3);
                   }
